What is worse fibroids or polyps?

17 Jul 2024, 00:00

Uterine fibroids are made up of thick muscle tissues while polyps are made from endometrial tissues (lining of the uterus). Thus, polyps are more dangerous than uterine fibroids as they lead to serious health issues that include vaginal bleeding, bladder issues, abnormal menses, and even cancer. Are polyps or fibroids cancerous? Both types of growth can cause heavy periods, irregular periods, or fertility issues, but fibroids are not, by definition, cancerous.

What's the difference between Annyeong and Annyeonghaseyo?

09 Jul 2024, 00:00

What is the difference between 안녕 (annyeong) and 안녕하세요 (annyeonghaseyo)? 안녕하세요 (annyeonghaseyo) is the formal and polite way to greet someone. This is the phrase that is used most often with people. 안녕 (annyeong) is the informal version that is used with people you are close with. Is Annyeong hello or good bye? Annyeong (안녕) is a casual, informal way of saying "Hello". It is typically used among close friends and not people you have just met.
